<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бутылка.html>буты́лка</a> (643)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">butelka</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bouteille</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bottle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бутылка.html>буты́лка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">butýlka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бутылка.html>буты́лки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бутылка.html>буты́лки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бутылка.html>буты́лок</a></b>)
</p>

<p><b>бу<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>лоч<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буфер.html>бу́фер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">búfer</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буфер.html>бу́фера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буфер.html>буфера́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буфер.html>буферо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>buffer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:винтовой.html>винтова́я</a> сце́пка <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:буфер.html>буфера́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vintovája scépka i <b>buferá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>buffers</b> and chain coupler</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">на́трий-фосфа́тный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:буфер.html>бу́фер</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nátrij-fosfátnyj <b>búfer</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">phosphate-<b>buffered</b> saline</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:буфер.html>бу́фер</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обмен.html>обме́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>búfer</b> obména</i> ― <span class="e-translation">clipboard (data buffer for copy and paste operations)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">переполне́ние <b><a href = vnd.unilang:буфер.html>бу́фера</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">perepolnénije <b>búfera</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>buffer</b> overflow</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">automotive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bumper <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">mechanical device to absorb impact</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> humorous<span class="ib-comma">,</span> usually in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> boob</li></ol>

***бухать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бухать.html>буха́ть</a> (16426)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*buxati</i>, originally onomatopoeic.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухать.html>бу́хать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">búxatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухнуть.html>бу́хнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to thump, to bang</li>
<li><i>cannons</i> to thunder, to thud</li>
<li>to let fall with a thud</li>
<li>to blurt out</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>According to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vladimir_Dal" class="extiw" title="w:Vladimir Dal">Vladimir Dal</a> it is related to the homograph <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухать.html>бу́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">búxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухать.html>буха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">buxátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухнуть.html>бухну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drink, to booze, to tipple</li></ol>

<p><b>бу́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>хать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:бухнуть.html>бу́хнуть</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бухнуть.html>бухну́ть</a> (14833)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухать.html>бу́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">búxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухнуть.html>бу́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">búxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухать.html>бу́хать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to thump, to bang</li>
<li>to thunder, to thud <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of cannons</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to let fall with a thud</li>
<li>to blurt out</li></ol>

<ul><li><i>See <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухать.html>бу́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">búxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for derived verbs.</i></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Same as 1.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухнуть.html>бу́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">búxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбухнуть.html>разбу́хнуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набухнуть.html>набу́хнуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">взбу́хнуть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to swell up, to swell</li></ol>

<p><b>бух<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ну́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. </p>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>бу́х<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>та</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).

<p>Derived from either <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буйный.html>бу́йный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bújnyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wild, unruly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухнуть.html>бу́хнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">búxnutʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to beat heavily</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">buszować</i>.

<p><b>бу<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:нить.html>нить</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. </p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:производный.html>Произво́дное</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:буян.html>буя́н</a></b> ➔ бу + <b>ян</b> + <b><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></b> + ть (суффиксальный).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-бу-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-ян-и</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***бы.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> (37)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The word was the third-person singular aorist of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bytʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, an otherwise obsolete Russian tense (see <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">бꙑти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">byti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">by</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">A verbal particle used to render conditional and subjunctive patterns</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́л</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja govoríl.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I spoke.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́л</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>by</b> govoríl.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I would (should) have spoken.; I would speak.; I might speak.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The particle <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a></b> is often shortened to <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">б</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">b</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li>
<li>The particle <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a></b> may come before or after the verb it is targeting.</li>
<li>The particle <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a></b> is often omitted in colloquial settings. For example:</li></ul>
<dl><dd><ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:словно.html>сло́вно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> → <a href = vnd.unilang:словно.html>сло́вно</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a>)</li></ul></dd></dl>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:частица.html>Части́ца</a>; неизменяемое, безударн., <a href = vnd.unilang:употребляться.html>употребля́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обычно.html>обы́чно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лами</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> прош. <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> инфинитиве.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-бы-</b>.
</p>

***бывалый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бывалый.html>быва́лый</a> (9670)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps derived from the past tense of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">byvátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to take place, to happen, to be (regularly)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бывалый.html>быва́лый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">byvályj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> worldly-wise, experienced
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бывалый.html>быва́лый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:солдат.html>солда́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>byvályj</b> soldát</i> ― <span class="e-translation">veteran</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> habitual, familiar
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бывалый.html>быва́лое</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto délo <b>byváloje</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this is nothing new</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Short forms <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">*<a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́л</a>, *<a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́ла</a>, *<a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́ло</a>, *<a href = vnd.unilang:бывалый.html>быва́лы</a></span> theoretically exist, but are usually avoided due to their similarity to past-tense forms (compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́л</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">byvál</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">it took place, it happened, he was (regularly)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, feminine <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́ла</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">byvála</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:быдло.html>бы́дло</a> (20974)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">bydło</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быдло.html>бы́дло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">býdlo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быдло.html>бы́дла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быдло.html>бы́дла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быдло.html>бы́дл</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cattle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rabble; uncultured or stupid people</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sheeple</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>бы́д<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ло</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><b>бы́д<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ло</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-быдл-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-о</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бык.html>бык</a> (3779)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bykъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бык.html>бык</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">byk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бык.html>быка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бык.html>быки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бык.html>быко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bull, ox</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a big, strong, or stubborn man</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gangster, mobster, soldier <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">rank-and-file member of a criminal gang</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> abutment, pier</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">быстренький</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bystrenʹkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быстро.html>бы́стро</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">býstro</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-еньк</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-enʹk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
